       <div class="module module__lead" data-module="lead">
        <article class="article article--lead" data-article-id="Y3JES3UAJFCEDO4NKHVQPZH3J4" data-ga-content-type="article" data-ga-module="life_and_culture" data-ga-section="life_and_culture" data-ga-url="https://www.oregonlive.com/travel/2021/03/head-to-oregons-high-desert-for-a-spring-break-with-open-spaces.html" data-image-thumb="https://www.oregonlive.com/resizer/_7Q2gnXZ5mlElIoBv3FI2iTD8RA=/300x225/smart/cloudfront-us-east-1.images.arcpublishing.com/advancelocal/LDYMUAUYMFEVNFBBO2NUCNGPHU.jpg" data-module="life_and_culture" data-publishedon="1616337000" data-section="life_and_culture" data-section-name="life_and_culture" data-social-hed="Head to Oregon’s high desert for a spring break with open spaces" data-source="https://www.oregonlive.com/travel/2021/03/head-to-oregons-high-desert-for-a-spring-break-with-open-spaces.html" data-type="article" id="article-Y3JES3UAJFCEDO4NKHVQPZH3J4">

         </div>
         <div class="article__label-wrap">
          <span class="article__label">
           Travel &amp; Outdoors
          </span>
         </div>
         <div class="article__details--headline">
          <h1>
           <a data-ga-content-type="article" data-linktype="headline" href="https://www.oregonlive.com/travel/2021/03/head-to-oregons-high-desert-for-a-spring-break-with-open-spaces.html">
            Head to Oregon’s high desert for a spring break with open spaces
           </a>
          </h1>
         </div>
         <div class="article__details">
          <div class="article__details--summary">
           If you need a little extra space this spring, look no further than Oregon’s high desert.
          </div>
          <div class="article__details--byline">
           <span>
            <span>
             Jamie Hale
            </span>
            ,
            <time class="" datetime="1616311800">
             5h ago
            </time>

       <div class="module module__auto-fill" id="auto-secondary">
        <article class="article" data-article-id="22DXB2PKPBFKHKY6QNQC7DRTUA" data-ga-content-type="article" data-ga-module="life_and_culture" data-ga-section="life_and_culture" data-ga-url="https://www.oregonlive.com/dining/2021/03/fueled-by-viral-tiktok-trends-downtown-portlands-toki-is-a-new-destination-from-the-han-oak-team-takeout-diaries.html" data-image-thumb="https://www.oregonlive.com/resizer/3UMexz1ToLAcwKYggfrzbkBR-Hs=/300x225/smart/cloudfront-us-east-1.images.arcpublishing.com/advancelocal/UQKH4TWBMNFTDIYZCCJU2FNKZI.JPG" data-module="life_and_culture" data-publishedon="1616259770" data-section="life_and_culture" data-section-name="life_and_culture" data-social-hed="Fueled by TikTok trends, Toki is a new downtown destination from the Han Oak team" data-source="https://www.oregonlive.com/dining/2021/03/fueled-by-viral-tiktok-trends-downtown-portlands-toki-is-a-new-destination-from-the-han-oak-team-takeout-diaries.html" data-type="article" id="article-22DXB2PKPBFKHKY6QNQC7DRTUA">
         <div class="article__picture article-picture--container">
         </div>
